<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:гастролировать.html>гастроли́ровать</a> (30307)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гастроль.html>гастро́ль</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gastrólʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ровать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-írovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гастролировать.html>гастроли́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gastrolírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to tour, to be on tour, to perform/play on tour</li>

***гать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:гать.html>гать</a> (16783)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*gatь</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гать.html>гать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гать.html>га́ти</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гать.html>га́ти</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гать.html>га́тей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>a causeway through swamps, made from logs or brushwood, a corduroy road</li></ol>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Hauptwache</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">main guardhouse</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гауптвахта.html>гауптва́хта</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gauptváxta</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гауптвахта.html>гауптва́хты</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гауптвахта.html>гауптва́хты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гауптвахта.html>гауптва́хт</a></b>)

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a guardhouse with an area for line-up of guards</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a chief guard of a city or a garrison</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гвоздика.html>гвозди́ка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gvozdíka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гвоздика.html>гвозди́ки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гвоздика.html>гвозди́ки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гвоздика.html>гвозди́к</a></b>)
</p>

<li><i>spice</i> cloves</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:гвоздь.html>гвоздь</a> (2418)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*gvozdь</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гвоздь.html>гвоздь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gvozdʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гвоздь.html>гвоздя́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гвоздь.html>гво́зди</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гвоздь.html>гвозде́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>nail, tack, peg <i>(construction)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гвоздь.html>гвоздь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:программа.html>програ́ммы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">gvozdʹ prográmmy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the highlight of the program, high spot</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***где.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:где.html>где</a> (69)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">къдѣ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kŭdě</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, alteration of <span class="Cyrs" lang="orv">къде</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="tr Latn">kŭde</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> with the locative ending -ѣ, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kъde</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_2">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:где.html>где</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gde</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>where
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:где.html>Где</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>мои́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сапог.html>сапоги́</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Gde</b> moí sapogí?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Where are my boots?</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Conjunction_2">Conjunction</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:где.html>где</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gde</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>where
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>зна́ю</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:где.html>где</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>мои́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сапог.html>сапоги́</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja ne znáju, <b>gde</b> moí sapogí.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I don’t know where my boots are.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гей.html>гей</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gej</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гей.html>ге́я</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гей.html>ге́и</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гей.html>ге́ев</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li class="senseid" id="Russian-a_male_homosexual"><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a male homosexual; gay</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:геморрой.html>геморро́й</a> (19283)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:геморрой.html>геморро́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gemorrój</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:геморрой.html>геморро́я</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:геморрой.html>геморро́и</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:геморрой.html>геморро́ев</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">pathology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> hemorrhoid, hemorrhoids</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> problem, difficulty, pain in the ass

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:генералитет.html>генералите́т</a> (31339)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Generalität</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:генералитет.html>генералите́т</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">generalitét</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:генералитет.html>генералите́та</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:генералитет.html>генералите́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:генералитет.html>генералите́тов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military<span class="ib-comma">,</span> collective</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> supreme command, generals</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> higher authorities</li></ol>
